       <article id="post-84" class="clearfix post-84 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-programming category-tutorials tag-api tag-flac tag-google tag-python tag-speech-recognition xfolkentry"> 
        <h1 class="entry-title">Python Google Speech to Text API implementation</h1> 
        <div class="entry-meta">
          by 
         <span class="vcard author"><span class="fn"><a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/author/tpayton/" title="Posts by Travis Payton" rel="author">Travis Payton</a></span></span>&nbsp;on&nbsp;
         <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/" class="time"><time class="date published updated" datetime="2014-09-07">September 7, 2014</time></a>&nbsp;in&nbsp;
         <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/topics/programming/" rel="category tag">Programming</a>, 
         <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/topics/tutorials/" rel="category tag">Tutorials</a>&nbsp;&nbsp;
         <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/#comments">15 Comments</a> 
        </div> 
        <div class="entry-content description clearfix"> 
         <p style="text-align: center;"><a href="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png" class="external" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><img data-attachment-id="88" data-permalink="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/speech-to-text-with-googles-api-logo-1/" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?fit=959%2C350" data-orig-size="959,350" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="Speech to Text with Googles API logo (1)" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?fit=300%2C109" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?fit=750%2C274" class="aligncenter wp-image-88 size-full" src="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?resize=750%2C274" alt="Using Google's Speech to Text API with Python to transcribe audio files" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?w=959 959w, https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?resize=300%2C109 300w, https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/Speech-to-Text-with-Googles-API-logo-1.png?resize=728%2C265 728w" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> 
         <p>This constantly seems to be a request on Stack Overflow, and the fact that documentation for Googles Speech API is practically non-existent, I have decided to share an implementation of it with everyone. &nbsp;If you just want the source code <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/gsst.zip">here you go</a>.</p> 
         <h2>Google Speech API Supported File Types</h2> 
         <p>First off, your audio must first be encoded in the <a href="https://xiph.org/flac/" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">FLAC</a> audio format for Googles Speech API to accept it. &nbsp;We will not be&nbsp;transcoding audio in the Python script, so you will have to do it before hand. If you need an&nbsp;easy to use tool to convert your audio files, give <a href="http://www.freac.org" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">fre:ac</a> a try. &nbsp;It is a free, open-source, converter for Windows, Mac OS X, Linux, and FreeBSD. &nbsp;Alright now on to the good stuff.</p> 
         <h3>FLAC&nbsp;Basics</h3> 
         <p>It is really useful to be able to pull out some information from our FLAC&nbsp;files with the Python script so that we dont have to worry about a 3rd Party library or application. &nbsp;Luckily for us, FLAC&nbsp;is an open source format&nbsp;with really clear specifications. &nbsp;The only information we really need to extract can all be found in the <a href="https://xiph.org/flac/format.html#metadata_block_streaminfo" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">STREAMINFO METADATA_BLOCK</a>. &nbsp;The basic diagram of what we need out of the&nbsp;FLAC&nbsp;file looks like this:</p> 
         <p><a href="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png" class="external" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><img data-attachment-id="97" data-permalink="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/flac-file-overview/" data-orig-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?fit=960%2C753" data-orig-size="960,753" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="fLaC file overview" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?fit=300%2C235" data-large-file="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?fit=750%2C588" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-97" src="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?resize=750%2C588" alt="fLaC file overview" srcset="https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?w=960 960w, https://i0.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/fLaC-file-overview.png?resize=300%2C235 300w" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> 
         <p>The first METADATA_BLOCK is ALWAYS the STREAM_INFO block. &nbsp;The first bit in the METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER simply marks whether this METADATA_BLOCK is the last one. &nbsp;The next 7 bits mark the BLOCK_TYPE, and then the last 24 bits mark the length of METADATA to follow the header.</p> 
         <p><a href="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png" class="external" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><img data-attachment-id="98" data-permalink="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/metadata_block_header/" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=955%2C411" data-orig-size="955,411" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=300%2C129" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=750%2C323" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-98" src="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?resize=750%2C323" alt="METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?w=955 955w, https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?resize=300%2C129 300w" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a></p> 
         <p>So that should be easy enough to at least get started with confirming that the file we send to our script is&nbsp;actually a FLAC file. &nbsp;Lets see if we can start reading some info from FLAC files</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d973769899b882100886" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

    flacBits = f.read(4)  # Get the Magic Number
    if flacBits != "fLaC":
        print "not a fLaC file!"
        # We should quit now and return the error
    flacBits = f.read(1)  # Get the first 8 bits of the STREAMINFO METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER
    if ord(flacBits) == 0:  # STREAMINFO BLOCK FOUND!!
        # do some more stuff...</textarea>

         <p></p> 
         <p>Pretty easy right? &nbsp;the python <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/functions.html#ord" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">ord()</a> function returns the number&nbsp;of a byte string  the inverse of <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/functions.html#chr" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">chr()</a> &nbsp;(which turns a&nbsp;number into an&nbsp;ASCII character). &nbsp;Since STREAMINFO is never the last block, the first 8 bits of the METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER should be 0s for the STREAMINFO block. 0 for the first bit, and 0s for the next 7 bits.</p> 
         <h3>STREAMINFO BLOCK</h3> 
         <p>So now that we can determine what is and is not a FLAC file, lets go ahead and start pulling out the information we need. &nbsp;We only need to tell Google the Sample Rate of the file, however since we are already here why dont we get as much information as possible.</p> 
         <p>The STREAMINFO_MEATADATA_BLOCK looks like this:</p> 
         <p><a href="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png" class="external" rel="nofollow" target="_blank"><img data-attachment-id="103" data-permalink="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/09/python-google-speech-api/streaminfo-metadata_block_header/" data-orig-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=860%2C518" data-orig-size="860,518" data-comments-opened="1" data-image-meta="{&quot;aperture&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;credit&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;camera&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;caption&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;created_timestamp&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;copyright&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;focal_length&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;iso&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;shutter_speed&quot;:&quot;0&quot;,&quot;title&quot;:&quot;&quot;,&quot;orientation&quot;:&quot;0&quot;}" data-image-title="STREAMINFO METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER" data-image-description="" data-medium-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=300%2C180" data-large-file="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?fit=750%2C452" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-103" src="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?resize=750%2C452" alt="STREAMINFO METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER" srcset="https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?w=860 860w, https://i1.wp.com/codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/STREAMINFO-METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER.png?resize=300%2C180 300w" sizes="(max-width: 750px) 100vw, 750px" data-recalc-dims="1"></a>So going through and parsing this block of data is pretty straight forward. Lets go ahead and just store the information&nbsp;as we go through them. &nbsp;When it comes to handling raw binary data in Python, <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/struct.html" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">struct</a> is a very useful library! &nbsp;We should use it! The most useful feature will be the <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/struct.html#struct.unpack" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">unpack()</a> method. &nbsp;Make sure you consult the <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/struct.html#format-characters" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Format Characters</a> chart if youre not sure what they mean. &nbsp;All numbers are big-endian, so we are using the &gt; character before our Format Characters.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989ab654588624" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
from struct import *

with open("test.flac", "rb") as f:
    flacBits = f.read(4)  # Get the Magic Number
    if flacBits != "fLaC":
        print "not a fLaC flacBits!"
    flacBits = f.read(1)  # Get the STREAMINFO METADATA_BLOCK_HEADER
    if ord(bytes) == 0:  # STREAMINFO BLOCK FOUND!!
        # Parse the STREMINFO BLOCK
        minBlockSize, maxBlockSize = unpack('&gt;HH', flacBits.read(4)) 
        minFrameSize = unpack('&gt;I', '\x00' + flacBits.read(3))
        FrameSize = unpack('&gt;I', '\x00' + flacBits.read(3))
        sampleInfo = flacBits.read(8)
        sampleInfoBytes = unpack('&gt;Q', sampleInfo)[0]
        sampleRate = sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 44
        channels = ((sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 41) &amp; 7) + 1
        bitsperSample = ((sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 36) &amp; 0x1F) + 1
        length = (sampleInfoBytes &amp; 0x0000000FFFFFF) / float(sampleRate)</textarea>
          </div>

              <td class="crayon-code">
               <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d97376989ab654588624-1">
                 <span class="crayon-st">from</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-k ">struct</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-r">import</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>

         <p></p> 
         <p>Thats all the information we need from the FLAC file, how about we turn this into a <strong>Class</strong> so that it is easier to use. &nbsp;We will rename some things as well as add some error messages so we can catch errors before trying to send the file to Google.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989b1920986138" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
class fLaC_Reader(object):
    error = ""
    sampleRate = 0
    channels = 0
    bitsperSample = 0
    length = 0.0
    minBlockSize, maxBlockSize = 0, 0

    def __init__(self, file):
        bytes = file.read(4)  # get Magic Number
        if bytes != "fLaC":
            self.error += "Not a fLaC file! Aborting\n"
        bytes = file.read(1)  # Get STREAMINFO metadata Block Header
        if ord(bytes) == 0:  # "STREAMINFO BLOCK FOUND"
        # Jump to the STREAMINFO Block, 24 bits from here.
            file.read(3)
        # parse STREMINFO BLOCK
            self.minBlockSize, self.maxBlockSize = unpack('&gt;HH', file.read(4))
            self.minFrameSize = unpack('&gt;I', '\x00' + file.read(3))
            self.FrameSize = unpack('&gt;I', '\x00' + file.read(3))
            if self.minBlockSize &lt; 16 or self.maxBlockSize &lt; 16:
                self.error += "Invalid Block Size! Aborting!\n"
                # if minBlockSize == maxBlockSize:
                # print "Fixed Blocksize: %d samples" % maxBlockSize
            sampleInfo = file.read(8)
            sampleInfoBytes = unpack('&gt;Q', sampleInfo)[0]
            self.sampleRate = sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 44
            self.channels = ((sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 41) &amp; 7) + 1
            self.bitsperSample = ((sampleInfoBytes &gt;&gt; 36) &amp; 0x1F) + 1
            self.length = (sampleInfoBytes &amp; 0x0000000FFFFFF) / float(self.sampleRate)

        else:
            self.error += "STREAMINFO BLOCK not first\n"</textarea>
          </div>

              <td class="crayon-code">
               <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d97376989b1920986138-1">
                 <span class="crayon-t">class</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-e">fLaC_Reader</span>

         <p>Perfect, now to get all of the information about a FLAC&nbsp;file we can call the class like this on the files object</p>

         <p></p> 
         <h2>Google Speech to Text API Basics</h2> 
         <p>Now that we can get the information we need out of a FLAC file, we can send it to Google for transcription. &nbsp;There exist a couple of endpoints for the Google Speech to Text API; we will be using Googles full-duplex API. &nbsp;The full-duplex version does not have a limit on&nbsp;file size, or length, and is what Chrome uses for their fancy&nbsp;<a href="https://www.google.com/intl/en/chrome/demos/speech.html" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Web Speech API</a>. &nbsp;The only problem with the full-duplex one is it does require an API key to use, and can be a little tricky due to the fact that Google has not made ANY documentation available for it. &nbsp;For more details about the other API endpoints, or how to get an API key, see my <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/2014/03/google-speech-recognition-api-information-guidelines/" title="Google Speech Recognition - API Information &amp; Guidelines">earlier post</a> about it.</p> 
         <p>The steps to call Googles Speech to Text API are</p> 
         <ul> 
          <li>Connect the Download stream &nbsp;https://www.google.com/speech-api/full-duplex/v1/down 
           <ul> 
            <li>Parameters: 
             <ul> 
              <li><strong>pair</strong></li> 
             </ul> </li> 
           </ul> </li> 
          <li>Connect the Upload stream  &nbsp;https://www.google.com/speech-api/full-duplex/v1/up 
           <ul> 
            <li>Parameters: 
             <ul> 
              <li><strong>key</strong>: API Key</li> 
              <li><strong>pair</strong>: A random string of Letters and Numbers used to join&nbsp;to the Upload stream</li> 
              <li><strong>lang</strong>: What language i.e. en-US</li> 
              <li><strong>continuous</strong>: keep the connections open</li> 
              <li><strong>interim</strong>: send back information as it becomes available (before final: true)</li> 
              <li><strong>pFilter*</strong>: Profanity filter (0: none, 1: some, 2: strict)</li> 
              <li>There are a lot of other options like <strong>grammar</strong>&nbsp;for specifying a particular grammar engine. &nbsp;To be honest, I have no idea what grammars are available.</li> 
             </ul> </li> 
           </ul> </li> 
          <li>Upon successful connection, Google will send back an empty result:&nbsp;<strong>{result:[]}</strong></li> 
          <li>Keep the Download &amp; Upload stream open until Google Finishes responding</li> 
          <li>Google will signal the transcription&nbsp;is finished with a f<strong>inal: true</strong> tag in the JSON&nbsp;object 
           <ul> 
            <li><span style="color: #993300;">Files with long silences in them will have multiple <strong>final: true</strong> sections returned!</span></li> 
            <li>Google will also send a response to the Upload stream connection to signal there is nothing else to process</li> 
           </ul> </li> 
          <li>Close the Upload Stream</li> 
          <li>Close the Download Stream</li> 
         </ul> 
         <p>The tricky part is getting the Download and Upload streams to function simultaneously and asynchronously. Sounds like a perfect job for Python <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/threading.html#thread-objects" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Threads</a> and the incredibly useful <a href="http://docs.python-requests.org/en/latest/" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Requests</a> library!</p> 
         <p>Lets go ahead and start with putting this into a&nbsp;<strong>Class&nbsp;</strong>as well. &nbsp;We will need to store the result in an array in case our audio file has a large gap of silence between audio, as Google will send multiple transcriptions for each part. &nbsp;We can use our fLaC_Reader class to pull out the information we need as well. &nbsp;For the Upstream, we also need to set a Content-Type header with the value of audio/x-flac; rate=OUR SAMPLE RATE. &nbsp;If the rate does not match the file, then Google will send back some very strange results as they do not process it correctly</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989c1217525035" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>

          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
class GoogleSpeechAPI(object):
    result = ''
    length = 0
    sampleRate = 0

    def __init__(self, file):
        self.result = []
        self.file = file
        self.flac = fLaC_Reader(file)
        self.length = self.flac.length
        self.sampleRate = self.flac.sampleRate
        self.upstream_url = "https://www.google.com/speech-api/full-duplex/v1/up?key=%(key)s&amp;pair=%(pair)s&amp;lang=en-US&amp;client=chromium&amp;continuous&amp;interim&amp;pFilter=0"
        self.upstream_headers = {'content-type': 'audio/x-flac; rate=' + str(self.flac.sampleRate)}
        self.downstream_url = "https://www.google.com/speech-api/full-duplex/v1/down?pair=%(pair)s"
        self.api_key = "ENTER YOUR API KEY HERE"
        self.timeSinceResponse = 0
        self.response = ""
        self.connectionSuccessful = False
        self.no_result = False</textarea>
          </div>

def gen_data(self):
        while True:
            item = self.file.read((self.flac.minBlockSize * self.flac.bitsperSample) / 8)
            if item:
                yield item
            else:
                if self.no_result or self.timeSinceResponse &gt; 2:
                    return #Google is Done Responding, close UpStream
                time.sleep(.5)
                self.timeSinceResponse += .5
                yield "00000000"</textarea>

         </div> 
         <p></p> 
         <p>It goes through the file in manageable blocks based on the BlockSize and bitsperSample, making it a multiple of 8. &nbsp;Once it is done uploading, since we cant easily check the upstream for a response from Google we can use the interim results being returned from Google to gauge when Google is done with the file. If we dont hear anything after 2 seconds after Google has started sending results, its pretty safe to assume were done. &nbsp;In the meantime, we need to keep the Upstream open by sending Google dummy data. In this case its just a string of 8 zeros.</p> 
         <p>The last helper function we need is one to help us check if a response is a&nbsp;<strong>final:true</strong> response.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989d0308935432" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
def final(self):
        try:
          response = json.loads(self.response)
          if response['result']:
              if 'final' in response['result'][0]:
                  return response['result'][0]['final']
        except Exception, e:
          # assuming invalid JSON 
          return False  
        return False</textarea>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-main" style=""> 
           <table class="crayon-table"> 
            <tbody>
             <tr class="crayon-row">

         </div> 
         <p></p> 
         <p>Okay. &nbsp;Now to the controlling the Threading and the Upload and Download streams. &nbsp;How about a function aptly named start()? This will kick off the threads for the Upload and Download streams. It will also close the threads once the streams are finished. &nbsp;We are using a&nbsp;Request Sessions for each Thread, as a Session is not Thread safe although it usually works most of the time if you use only one Session for both the upstream and downstream. &nbsp;We can also skip the whole hassle of sending the file to Google if its not a valid FLAC file.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989d5506330495" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
def start(self):
        if self.flac.error != "":
            self.result = self.flac.error
            return
        pair = self.getPair()
        upstream_url = self.upstream_url % {"pair": pair, "key": self.api_key}
        downstream_url = self.downstream_url % {"pair": pair, "key": self.api_key}
        self.file.seek(0)
        self.upsession = requests.Session()
        self.downsession = requests.Session()
        self.upstream_thread = Thread(target=self.upstream, args=(upstream_url,))
        self.downstream_thread = Thread(target=self.downstream, args=(downstream_url,))

        self.downstream_thread.start()
        self.upstream_thread.start()

        self.stop()</textarea>

         <p></p> 
         <p>The stop() function is simple. &nbsp;We call <strong>join()</strong> on both of the threads. &nbsp;<strong>Join()</strong> will simply wait for the threads to finish, and then close them. &nbsp;The rest of the python script will wait for the Join() to finish before executing the next line. &nbsp;So we can actually time how long Google takes to Transcribe an audio file.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989da161131086" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

         <p></p> 
         <p>Okay, now for the upstream process. &nbsp;Using requests, its pretty simple. &nbsp; We dont need to capture any of the results of the upstream connection, but we should automatically&nbsp;retry if the connection is unsuccessful:</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989de727227433" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">

        result = self.upsession.post(url, headers=self.upstream_headers, data=self.gen_data())

         </div> 
         <p></p> 
         <p>The Downstream is a little more complicated. We are going to be mimicking the Deterministic Finite Automata that Chrome uses for interacting with the Speech API, but&nbsp;in a much more basic and crude way. &nbsp;We need to know what state we are in, 1. Not Connected, 2. Successful Connection, 3. If we have received a second empty response after a Successful Connection, &nbsp;4. If we have started receiving responses, and 5. If we have a final result. &nbsp;With the <strong>stream=True</strong> parameter we can access the responses as they come with the&nbsp;<strong>iter_lines()</strong> method. &nbsp;We store the response in the self.response variable, as that is what the self.final() function checks. If its a final result we add it to our results, and keep going. Our Downstream will keep listening for responses&nbsp;until the Upstream is closed. The upstream will only close when the Downstream quits receiving responses. &nbsp;So every time we get a result back from Google we reset the timer to keep the Upload stream going. &nbsp;If we dont hear anything for 2 seconds, the Upstream is closed, and the Downstream finishes.&nbsp;Pretty cool huh? &nbsp;Just like the upstream we are also going to restart the connection if it was unable to connect.</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989e3696619738" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
def downstream(self, url):
        r = self.downsession.get(url, stream=True)
        self.status_code = r.status_code
        if r.status_code == 200:
            for line in r.iter_lines():
                self.timeSinceResponse = 0
                self.response = line
                if line == '{"result":[]}':
                    # Google sends back an empty result signifying a successful connection
                    if not self.connectionSuccessful:
                        self.connectionSuccessful = True
                    else: # another empty response means Google couldn't find anything in the audio ...
                        # Make the result pretty / match normal results
                        self.result.append('{"result":[{"alternative":[{"transcript":"","confidence":0.99999}],"final":true}],"result_index":0}')
                        self.no_result = True
                if self.final():
                    self.result.append(line)
                    self.response = ""
        else:
            self.start()</textarea>
          </div>

class Timer:
    def __enter__(self):
        self.start = time.clock()
        return self

    def __exit__(self, *args):
        self.end = time.clock()
        self.interval = self.end - self.start</textarea>

                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-k ">struct</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-r">import</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-o">*</span>
                </div>
                <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d97376989ec521122639-5">
                 <span class="crayon-r">import</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-k ">time</span>
                </div>
                <div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-59d97376989ec521122639-6">
                 <span class="crayon-r">import</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-v">requests</span>
                 <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                 <span class="crayon-c"># External Library http://docs.python-requests.org/en/latest/user/install/#install</span>
                </div>
               </div></td> 
             </tr> 
            </tbody>
           </table> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
         <p></p> 
         <p>Now I can simply open a file, start the transcription, and time it!</p> 
         <p></p> 
         <div id="crayon-59d97376989f1136600294" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
          <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
           <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
           <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
            <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>

            <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">

            <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
             <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
            </div>
            <span class="crayon-language">Python</span>
           </div>
          </div> 
          <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
          <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
           <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
with open("test.flac", 'rb') as f:
    result = GoogleSpeechAPI(f)
    print "Audio is %.03f seconds long" % result.length
    f.seek(0)
    with Timer() as t:
        result.start()
    print "Result took %.03f sec" % t.interval
    print result.result</textarea>
          </div>

         <p>Well, I hope you found this tutorial enlightening. &nbsp;Special thanks go out to the <a href="https://src.chromium.org/viewvc/chrome/trunk/src/content/browser/speech/" class="external external_icon" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">Chromium Project</a> for making all of their code available ?</p> 
         <p>&nbsp;</p> 
         <p>Here is the complete <a href="http://codeabitwiser.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/09/gsst.zip">source code /&nbsp;working example</a> (minus an API key).</p>

         <p>Happy Transcribing!</p>

               <p>My flac I had: o meu carro é amarelo (pt-PT) equals my car is yellow (en-US)<br> Results Google Speech: [{result:[{alternative:[{transcript:o meu carro \xc3\xa9 amarelo,confidence:0.71846169}],final:true}],result_index:0}]</p>

               <div class="comment-avatar"> 
                <img alt="" src="https://0.gravatar.com/avatar/f73e8f9676a21e2279495f52786d3e60?s=60&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg" srcset="http://0.gravatar.com/avatar/f73e8f9676a21e2279495f52786d3e60?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=pg 2x" class="avatar avatar-60 photo" height="60" width="60"> 
               </div> 
               <div class="comment-content"> 
                <div class="comment-author"> 
                 <a href="http://travispayton.com" rel="external nofollow" class="url external external_icon" target="_blank">Travis Payton</a> 
                </div> 
                <div class="comment-meta">
                  May 16, 2015 at 1:16 pm 
                </div> 
                <div class="comment-text"> 
                 <p>Hi romao,</p> 
                 <p>You shouldnt need the # coding: utf-8  on the first line. The library is handling all of the unicode correctly, its just the final output function that I wrote wasnt really setup for Unicode or for anything other than a quick glance at the contents of the audio. The reason it is printing with the hex values of the unicode characters is it is actually printing a list / array of strings. Google will send back multiple results if there are large gaps of silence in your audio, these separate results are each stored in the result array. If you print a single element from the list then youll see that the unicode is displayed correctly, i.e. <code>print result.result[0]</code> Here is a cleaner way to get the final output as a JSON object in case you still need to manipulate it later, or would like to be able to read it because it contains unicode:</p> 
                 <p>Simply add / update this at the bottom of the main function<br> <code></code></p>
                 <code> <p></p> 
                  <div id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181" class="crayon-syntax crayon-theme-classic crayon-font-monaco crayon-os-pc print-yes notranslate" data-settings=" minimize scroll-mouseover" style=" margin-top: 12px; margin-bottom: 12px; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;"> 
                   <div class="crayon-toolbar" data-settings=" mouseover overlay hide delay" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
                    <span class="crayon-title"></span> 
                    <div class="crayon-tools" style="font-size: 12px !important;height: 18px !important; line-height: 18px !important;">
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-nums-button" title="Toggle Line Numbers">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-plain-button" title="Toggle Plain Code">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-wrap-button" title="Toggle Line Wrap">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-expand-button" title="Expand Code">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-copy-button" title="Copy">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="crayon-button crayon-popup-button" title="Open Code In New Window">
                      <div class="crayon-button-icon"></div>
                     </div>
                    </div>
                   </div> 
                   <div class="crayon-info" style="min-height: 16.8px !important; line-height: 16.8px !important;"></div> 
                   <div class="crayon-plain-wrap">
                    <textarea wrap="soft" class="crayon-plain print-no" data-settings="dblclick" readonly style="-moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4; font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important;">
print "Result took %.03f sec" % t.interval
# clean up results into JSON String
JSONResult = '['
for x in result.result:
    JSONResult += x + ' , '
JSONResult = JSONResult[:-3] + ']'
print JSONResult
writer.writerow([flac, result.length, result.sampleRate, JSONResult, t.interval])</textarea>
                   </div>

                         </div>
                        </div> </td> 
                       <td class="crayon-code">
                        <div class="crayon-pre" style="font-size: 12px !important; line-height: 15px !important; -moz-tab-size:4; -o-tab-size:4; -webkit-tab-size:4; tab-size:4;">
                         <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-1">
                          <span class="crayon-i">print</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-s">"Result took %.03f sec"</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-o">%</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-v">t</span>

                          <span class="crayon-v">interval</span>
                         </div>
                         <div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-2">
                          <span class="crayon-p"># clean up results into JSON String</span>
                         </div>
                         <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-3">
                          <span class="crayon-v">JSONResult</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-o">=</span>

                          <span class="crayon-s">'['</span>
                         </div>
                         <div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-4">
                          <span class="crayon-st">for</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>

                          <span class="crayon-v">result</span>

                          <span class="crayon-v">result</span>
                          <span class="crayon-o">:</span>
                         </div>
                         <div class="crayon-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-5">
                          <span class="crayon-h">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>
                          <span class="crayon-v">JSONResult</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-o">+=</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>

                         </div>
                         <div class="crayon-line crayon-striped-line" id="crayon-59d973769a075547852181-6">
                          <span class="crayon-v">JSONResult</span>
                          <span class="crayon-h"> </span>
                          <span class="crayon-o">=</span>

                <div class="comment-text"> 
                 <p>Sorry, my comment is probably confusing we were LDS missionaries together in Otaru, Japan. He was my first companion (missionaries are always in companionships of two or three), and, as they are largely responsible for training you, your first companion always makes a big impression on how you serve as a missionary. We would always joke about your trainer being your father because the influence is so profound.</p> 
                 <p>I was really, really lucky to have Travis as a trainerhe was really well-known in the mission for loving the people he served unconditionally, and I did my best to emulate that.</p> 
                 <p>Its pure coincidence (hence my shock) that we both happen to work on the same sort of problems professionally.</p>

					} else {
						frame.src = "http://jetpack.wordpress.com/jetpack-comment/?blogid=65576981&postid=84&comment_registration=0&require_name_email=0&stc_enabled=1&stb_enabled=1&show_avatars=1&avatar_default=mystery&greeting=Leave+a+Reply&greeting_reply=Leave+a+Reply+to+%25s&color_scheme=transparent&lang=en_US&jetpack_version=5.4&sig=4378a9f779850171b30fa22980bfc2eb01ebcbf9#parent=http%3A%2F%2Fcodeabitwiser.com%2F2014%2F09%2Fpython-google-speech-api%2F";

				if ( 'undefined' !== typeof addComment ) {
					addComment._Jetpack_moveForm = addComment.moveForm;

					addComment.moveForm = function ( commId, parentId, respondId, postId ) {
						var returnValue = addComment._Jetpack_moveForm( commId, parentId, respondId, postId ),
							cancelClick, cancel;

						if ( false === returnValue ) {
							cancel = document.getElementById( 'cancel-comment-reply-link' );
							cancelClick = cancel.onclick;
							cancel.onclick = function () {
								var cancelReturn = cancelClick.call( this );
								if ( false !== cancelReturn ) {
									return cancelReturn;
								}

								if ( ! comm_par ) {
									return cancelReturn;
								}

								comm_par = 0;

								tellFrameNewParent();

								return cancelReturn;
							};
						}

						if ( comm_par == parentId ) {
							return returnValue;
						}

						comm_par = parentId;

						tellFrameNewParent();

						return returnValue;
					};
				}

				
				// Do the post message bit after the dom has loaded.
				document.addEventListener( 'DOMContentLoaded', function () {
					var iframe_url = "http:\/\/jetpack.wordpress.com";
					if ( window.postMessage ) {
						if ( document.addEventListener ) {
							window.addEventListener( 'message', function ( event ) {
								var origin = event.origin.replace( /^http:\/\//i, 'https://' );
								if ( iframe_url.replace( /^http:\/\//i, 'https://' ) !== origin ) {
									return;
								}
								jQuery( frame ).height( event.data );
							});
						} else if ( document.attachEvent ) {
							window.attachEvent( 'message', function ( event ) {
								var origin = event.origin.replace( /^http:\/\//i, 'https://' );
								if ( iframe_url.replace( /^http:\/\//i, 'https://' ) !== origin ) {
									return;
								}
								jQuery( frame ).height( event.data );
							});
						}
					}
				})
